msg:The name of this hotel sounds quite grand and has a good structure. In my opinion, it deserves the name. Let me tell you about my experience in the hotel. I arrived at the hotel at around 10 o'clock in the morning. First of all, the lobby decoration is quite luxurious and the front desk service is acceptable. I asked the front desk if I could upgrade when I checked in for the first time. The hotel said yes. I got to the room and found that not only was the bed ugly, but there was even hair on it. I thought it didn't matter and I wouldn't make a fuss with the hotel. As a result, I was even more shocked when I went to the bathroom. The two rolls of toilet paper were both used by the previous guest. When I was putting on the toilet seat mat, I smelled a strong smell of urine and there was a lot of dirt on the inner wall of the toilet. Is this the quality of a 500-dollar hotel? The mouthwash cup was also dirty and not disinfected, which resulted in me having no place to go to the bathroom. The public bathroom on the first floor was even dirtier. Later, I went to the bathroom in the mall. Because I specifically used my points to exchange for a fruit plate when booking, the one on the store was very different from the picture. Let me talk about the false advertising of the merchant: the booking page showed that there was a welcome gift and a night bed service, but there was none. I called the front desk to ask, and the front desk didn't know what the night bed service was. Finally, I complained to Ctrip, and the store argued that it was a new employee who didn't understand. As a result, the booking page now doesn't have these two services. I think this is the best proof that they are guilty and don't know how to do the night bed service. What's more infuriating is the following: After the complaint, a person from Tianjin who claimed to be the director of rooms called and said she would handle the matter. I said I was in a hurry to wash up, and she said she would change a room for you. I said yes, and she said there were only suites. I said I wanted my original room, and she said it was okay to upgrade you. I didn't expect that this would become her reason for shirking responsibility later! I told her that the room I was staying in should not be cleaned first, and she agreed as a proof. In the afternoon, a man who claimed to be the general manager's assistant came. As soon as he entered the room, he crossed his legs and said in a condescending manner, "Look, I upgraded your room and gave you a fruit plate." His expression and meaning meant, "What else do you want!" Finally, I had no choice but to complain to Ctrip. Ctrip went even further. A female supervisor actually attacked me personally and had a very bad attitude. When I told her, she said that I would handle this matter and it was up to me. What she meant was that you had no chance to complain to me. She argued with me for more than a minute. My heart felt very uncomfortable. I took some medicine and slept for a night. When I checked out, I went to my original room to take pictures and use them later for rights protection. As a result, the room director came and asked me impatiently what I was doing. I found that the mouthwash cup in the room was replaced with a clean one. Because I said I would report to the Health Bureau, the hotel's behavior was really speechless. Afterwards, I kept trying to communicate with the general manager of the hotel. The general manager of the hotel refused to communicate on the grounds that he was busy in a meeting. He had no respect for consumers. I would like to ask the complaint supervisor of Ctrip again, are you worthy of the salary that Ctrip gives you? I would also like to ask, are you worthy of the 500 yuan fee paid by the customer? I will defend my rights to the end! !
